\doxysubsection{함수 문서화}
\Hypertarget{astcenccli__image__load__store_8cpp_a46a5fd770b78f8512d65273a03d0b6dc}\index{astcenccli\_image\_load\_store.cpp@{astcenccli\_image\_load\_store.cpp}!copy\_scanline@{copy\_scanline}}
\index{copy\_scanline@{copy\_scanline}!astcenccli\_image\_load\_store.cpp@{astcenccli\_image\_load\_store.cpp}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{copy\_scanline()}{copy\_scanline()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenccli__image__load__store_8cpp_a46a5fd770b78f8512d65273a03d0b6dc} 
static void copy\+\_\+scanline (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dst}{, }\item[{const void \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{src}{, }\item[{int}]{pixel\+\_\+count}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{astcenccli__image__load__store_8cpp_af52e5c57922db5c38a2bbaf385fe805b}{scanline\+\_\+transfer}}}]{method}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Copy a scanline from a source file and expand to a canonical format. 

Outputs are always 4 component RGBA, stored as U8 (LDR) or FP16 (HDR).


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em dst} & The start of the line to store to. \\
\hline
 & {\em src} & The start of the line to load. \\
\hline
 & {\em pixel\+\_\+count} & The number of pixels in the scanline. \\
\hline
 & {\em method} & The conversion function. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{get\_output\_filename()}{get\_output\_filename()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenccli__image__load__store_8cpp_a317fd3791349a6509f4eda9eeacc1800} 
static std\+::string get\+\_\+output\+\_\+filename (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structastcenc__image}{astcenc\+\_\+image}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{img}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{filename}{, }\item[{unsigned int}]{index}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Functions for loading/storing uncompressed and compressed images. 

Determine the output file name to use for a sliced image write.


\begin{DoxyParams}{매개변수}
{\em img} & The source data for the image. \\
\hline
{\em filename} & The base name of the file to save. \\
\hline
{\em index} & The slice index to write.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{반환값}
The file name to use when saving the file. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenccli__image__load__store_8cpp_a36fb7c666f502f49e4d18cf130a7958d} 
int get\+\_\+output\+\_\+filename\+\_\+enforced\+\_\+bitness (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{filename}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Check if the output file type requires a specific bitness. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{매개변수}
{\em filename} & The file name, containing hte extension to check.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{반환값}
Valid values are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item -\/1 -\/ error -\/ unknown file type.
\item 0 -\/ no enforced bitness.
\item 8 -\/ enforced 8-\/bit UNORM.
\item 16 -\/ enforced 16-\/bit FP16. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{load\_dds\_uncompressed\_image@{load\_dds\_uncompressed\_image}!astcenccli\_image\_load\_store.cpp@{astcenccli\_image\_load\_store.cpp}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{load\_dds\_uncompressed\_image()}{load\_dds\_uncompressed\_image()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenccli__image__load__store_8cpp_a3e91d7c742d9854faf8bb5a28e729885} 
static \mbox{\hyperlink{structastcenc__image}{astcenc\+\_\+image}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} load\+\_\+dds\+\_\+uncompressed\+\_\+image (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{filename}{, }\item[{bool}]{y\+\_\+flip}{, }\item[{bool \&}]{is\+\_\+hdr}{, }\item[{unsigned int \&}]{component\+\_\+count}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Load an uncompressed DDS image using the local custom loader. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
 & {\em filename} & The name of the file to load. \\
\hline
 & {\em y\+\_\+flip} & Should the image be vertically flipped? \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em is\+\_\+hdr} & Is this an HDR image load? \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em component\+\_\+count} & The number of components in the data.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{반환값}
The loaded image data in a canonical 4 channel format, or {\ttfamily nullptr} on error. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

static \mbox{\hyperlink{structastcenc__image}{astcenc\+\_\+image}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} load\+\_\+image\+\_\+with\+\_\+stb (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{filename}{, }\item[{bool}]{y\+\_\+flip}{, }\item[{bool \&}]{is\+\_\+hdr}{, }\item[{unsigned int \&}]{component\+\_\+count}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Load an image using STBImage to provide the loader. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
 & {\em filename} & The name of the file to load. \\
\hline
 & {\em y\+\_\+flip} & Should the image be vertically flipped? \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em is\+\_\+hdr} & Is this an HDR image load? \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em component\+\_\+count} & The number of components in the data.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{반환값}
The loaded image data in a canonical 4 channel format, or {\ttfamily nullptr} on error. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenccli__image__load__store_8cpp_a10761592472e9cc4d632946459d00bee} 
bool load\+\_\+ktx\+\_\+compressed\+\_\+image (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{filename}{, }\item[{bool \&}]{is\+\_\+srgb}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structastc__compressed__image}{astc\+\_\+compressed\+\_\+image}} \&}]{img}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Load a KTX compressed image using the local custom loader. 

Load a compressed .ktx image.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
 & {\em filename} & The name of the file to load. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em is\+\_\+srgb} & {\ttfamily true} if this is an s\+RGB image, {\ttfamily false} otherwise. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em img} & The output image to populate.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{반환값}
{\ttfamily true} on error, {\ttfamily false} otherwise. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

static \mbox{\hyperlink{structastcenc__image}{astcenc\+\_\+image}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} load\+\_\+ktx\+\_\+uncompressed\+\_\+image (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{filename}{, }\item[{bool}]{y\+\_\+flip}{, }\item[{bool \&}]{is\+\_\+hdr}{, }\item[{unsigned int \&}]{component\+\_\+count}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Load an uncompressed KTX image using the local custom loader. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
 & {\em filename} & The name of the file to load. \\
\hline
 & {\em y\+\_\+flip} & Should the image be vertically flipped? \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em is\+\_\+hdr} & Is this an HDR image load? \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em component\+\_\+count} & The number of components in the data.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{반환값}
The loaded image data in a canonical 4 channel format, or {\ttfamily nullptr} on error. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{load\_ncimage()}{load\_ncimage()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenccli__image__load__store_8cpp_aff0de9c0d50e5630b61f0d6e597fcd65} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{structastcenc__image}{astcenc\+\_\+image}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} load\+\_\+ncimage (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{filename}{, }\item[{bool}]{y\+\_\+flip}{, }\item[{bool \&}]{is\+\_\+hdr}{, }\item[{unsigned int \&}]{component\+\_\+count}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Load uncompressed image. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
 & {\em filename} & The file path on disk. \\
\hline
 & {\em y\+\_\+flip} & Should this image be Y flipped? \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em is\+\_\+hdr} & Is the loaded image HDR? \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em component\+\_\+count} & The number of components in the loaded image.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{반환값}
The astc image file, or nullptr on error. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Save a KTX uncompressed image using a local store routine. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{매개변수}
{\em img} & The source data for the image. \\
\hline
{\em filename} & The name of the file to save. \\
\hline
{\em y\+\_\+flip} & Should the image be vertically flipped?\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{반환값}
{\ttfamily true} if the image saved OK, {\ttfamily false} on error. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
